DashboardSpecResource

(Appears on:DashboardSpec)

Field Description
id
string
dashboardLists
[]int64 		(Optional)

The list of dashboard lists this dashboard belongs to.
dashboardListsRemoved
[]int64 		(Optional)

The list of dashboard lists this dashboard should be removed from. Internal only.
description
string 		(Optional)

The description of the dashboard.
isReadOnly
bool 		(Optional)

Whether this dashboard is read-only.
layoutType
string

The layout type of the dashboard.
notifyList
[]string 		(Optional)

The list of handles of users to notify when changes are made to this dashboard.
reflowType
string 		(Optional)

The reflow type of a new dashboard layout. Set this only when layout type is ordered. If set to fixed, the dashboard expects all widgets to have a layout, and if it's set to auto, widgets should not have layouts.
restrictedRoles
[]string 		(Optional)

Role UUIDs corresponding to users authorized to edit the dashboard. This feature is currently in beta.
templateVariable
[]DashboardSpecTemplateVariable 		(Optional)

The list of template variables for this dashboard.
templateVariablePreset
[]DashboardSpecTemplateVariablePreset 		(Optional)

The list of selectable template variable presets for this dashboard.
title
string

The title of the dashboard.
url
string 		(Optional)

The URL of the dashboard.
widget
[]DashboardSpecWidget

The list of widgets to display on the dashboard.

string 		(Optional)
